<userid>108927309190141582381< /userid>< user_name>
Chase Slagle</user_name>
< Time>
1461174821423<//Time>
<Rating>4< /Rating>< review>
The travel agent at the Armed Forces Career Center told me that the cruises that were offered here would take me to some exotic locations. I mean, they weren't wrong....but the agent never mentioned all the cleaning and maintenance I would have to do on the way there.

Sleeping accommodations were expected to be the "economy" beds, which is all I could really afford at the time. Was shocked to find out I wouldn't be staying in staterooms that Carnival or Disney cruises boasts. On the plus-side; hearing the sound of the water on the other side of the 2" steel bulkhead was nice when trying to sleep.

They also assigned me to help out with a radar system during my cruise getaway, of which I think radiated me to the point of never producing another "Y" chromosome again in my life.

My cruise wouldn't be complete without mentioning the food. The agent mentioned having chefs onboard and cooked-to-order breakfasts. What I experienced was 52 ways that rice could be prepared, who knew!?!

Giving a 4-star review because after all that trouble I decided I should get an education (which they gave me as a consolation/parting gift) instead of going on another cruise.</review>

< review>
It's a Navy base, with a Starbucks, medium size NEX,  macdonalds, and one or two other food places. The base theater is also here, where they play free movies and you only have to pay for snacks. It is a really big base so it does get busy when work starts and wok ends. I'm on shore duty right now, so to workout, I have to go to the smaller base that's connected to it for the gym. It's seriously a 15 min walk on a bridge or a five minute drive. On the little base its connected to is where the barracks rooms are, along with gyms, a bowling alley, small NEX... If you're wondering if they have a big NEX, they do. It's like down the street from the main base. So it's kind of like three bases separated by like a busy street and train tracks, but they are all in walking distance or a less than five minute drive, depending on traffic.<//review>

<Rate>4</Rate><Review>Almost perfect.
My Quesadilla, made from masa de maiz (corn tortilla masa) and with Flor de Calabaza (squash blossoms) was amazing!  Their Quesadillas made with masa are completely different from the flour tortilla ones you're probably used to.  I suggest you give one a try!  Incidentally, they do have Quesadillas made from flour tortillas, so if you insist on that, you're good!
My mom tells me that her Birria de Chivo was perfect, served with chopped onions and cilantro and tortillas on the side.
My Torta was the only thing I had a small problem with.  I ordered a Torta made with Barbacoa de Res (beef, as opposed to the traditional lamb, which they also have) and was expecting my beef to be juicy with that awesome broth it's supposed to have.  Instead it was dry.  It had the consistency of carnitas, only dryer.  That made me a little disappointed.
Everything else about the Torta was delicious, though.  The bread was perfect, the beans and avacado were delicious, and the queso fresco (or panela, I'm not sure!) was a happy surprise!
I will definitely go again and try their other Quesadillas.  They have Ongos (mushrooms), and even Huitlacoche (can't describe, look it up!).  And I will try the Torta again, only this time with Al Pastor.  Can't go wrong with that!</Review><pictures>None<//pictures><response>None< /response>< gmapID>

<Review>It's okay!

The drive thru went into the street, and the wait time was long. About 10 minutes? 10 minutes to order, and then another 10 waiting for my food.

The soda was flat, and they had to check with me at the window what my order was, but at least they're making sure I don't leave without my food, so I greatly appreciate it!

The burger was still hot and delicious! I ordered the Buford, and it was just what I wanted!

The fries were soft, lukewarm, and kind of average tasting. They look really good with all that spice on em, but the crunch isn't satisfying, and the flavor is kind of bland.

I ordered mozzarella sticks, but they were out. I don't blame them, though, cause I came in at 9 pm xD

I also ordered the garlic chicken wings, which were SO good, the sauce actually tastes like it's made with real garlic, but the packaging is leaky. My home is only 10 minutes away, but the bottom of the bag was soaked with greasy sauce from the wings, and now I have this majorly huge, garlic-smelling grease stain on the front passenger seat of my car :/

It's definitely a place I'll revisit, but I don't think it's at the top of my list.< /Review><pics>None<//pics>< resp>

<user>103040860086789583660<//user><Name>Bryan Auza< /Name><date>1511056452134</date>< Rate>

< text>
It is a rarity that I stop in at a Rally's or Checkers. That very much is true. Another truth is that there are not many of them. That is perfectly fine by me, and it makes each visit worthwhile. I had the baconzilla combo. Bacon and cheese and the beef patty and the bun were very much as I remembered the last time I had it. Very straightforward. All stacked in a choreographed pile of goodness. My burger this time was no different. It had a good amount of bacon which provided the right amount of saltiness to compliment the beef patties and the melted cheese. The bacon had a good amount of crispiness too. The seasoned fries are a step above any other fast food restaurant standard french fries. Of course if you prefer seasoned fries. Which I do, and mine were done perfectly. I also had a strawberry smoothie that was very..... smooth with just the right amount of sweetness. Rally's and Checker's offer soft serve and other dessert items too. So on hot days it is worth checking out. Outside seating is only available. It is a very modern location and parking is available and well lit.</text>
